[30;1m32 | [0m[35mDuring a semantic analysis a parse tree is walked in the depth-first manner and[0m
[30;1m33 | [0m[35mfor each node a proper visitor method is called to transform it to some other[0m
[30;1m34 | [0m[35mform. The results are then fed to the parent node visitor method.  This is[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35mrepeated until the final, top level parse tree node is processed (its visitor is[0m
[30;1m36 | [0m[35mcalled). The result of the top level node is the final output of the semantic[0m
[30;1m37 | [0m[35manalysis.[0m

[30;1m11 | [0m[35mthe inner nodes are non-terminals.[0m

[30;1m101 | [0m[35mparse tree node with more than one child.[0m

[30;1m103 | [0m[35mAs a side note, there is implicit reduction of nodes whose grammar rule is a [0m
[30;1m104 | [0m[35msequence with only one child.[0m
